Ragdoll save-load stale transform contract deep audit

Goal:
  Prove where bhkRagdollController +0xA4 is populated, not only read.
  Prove whether save/load reuses a controller whose +0x48/+0x58/+0x2A4/+0xA4 belong to different generations.
  Identify the safe intervention point: skip update, rebuild controller, or clear owner ragdoll pointer.

Known before this script:
  Current Rust guard validates readability/nullness only. That catches NULL entries but not stale readable transforms.
  FUN_00C79680 reads bone_table[i]+0x34; FUN_00C75B40 and FUN_00C79A50 write transforms back into bone entries.
